    <body>

      <div n="4" type="sthāna">

        <head>cikitsāsthānaṃ</head>


        <div n="21" type="level2" subtype="adhyāya">
          <head>ekaviṃśatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ|</head>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.21.1"><label xml:lang="en">4.21.1</label> athātaḥ śūkadoṣacikitsitaṃ
            vyākhyāsyāmaḥ|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.21.2"><label xml:lang="en">4.21.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.21.3"><label xml:lang="en">4.21.3</label> saṃlikhya sarṣapīṃ samyak
            kaṣāyair avacūrṇayet | kaṣāyeṣv eva tailaṃ ca kurvīta vraṇaropaṇam|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.21.4"><label xml:lang="en">4.21.4</label> aṣṭhīlikāṃ jalaukobhir grāhayec ca
            punaḥ punaḥ | tathā cānupaśāmyantīṃ kaphagranthivad uddharet|| </l>




          <l xml:id="SS.4.21.5"><label xml:lang="en">4.21.5</label> svedayed grathitaṃ śaśvan nāḍīsvedena
            buddhimān |
            <caesura/>
             sukhoṣṇair upanāhaiś ca susnigdhair upanāhayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.21.6"><label xml:lang="en">4.21.6</label> kumbhīkāṃ pākamāpannāṃ
            bhindyāc chuddhāṃ tu ropayet |
            <caesura/>
             tailena triphalālodhratindukāmrātakena tu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.21.7"><label xml:lang="en">4.21.7</label> grāhayitvā jalaukobhir alajīṃ
            secayet tataḥ |
            <caesura/>
             kaṣāyais teṣu siddhaṃ ca tailaṃ ropaṇam iṣyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.21.8"><label xml:lang="en">4.21.8</label> balātailena koṣṇena mṛditaṃ
            pariṣecayet |
            <caesura/>
             bhadhuraiḥ sarpiṣā snigdhaiḥ sukhoṣṇair upanāhayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.21.9"><label xml:lang="en">4.21.9</label> saṃmūḍhapiḍakāṃ kṣipraṃ jalaukobhir
            upācaret |
            <caesura/>
             bhittvā paryāgatāṃ cāpi lepayet kṣaudrasarpiṣā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.21.10"><label xml:lang="en">4.21.10</label> avamanthe gate pākaṃ bhinne tailaṃ
            vidhīyate |
            <caesura/>
             dhavāśvakarṇapattaṅgasallakītindukīkṛtam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.21.11"><label xml:lang="en">4.21.11</label> kriyāṃ puṣkarikāyāṃ tu śītāṃ
            sarvāṃ prayojayet |
            <caesura/>
             jalaukobhir hareccāsṛk sarpiṣā cāvasecayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.21.12"><label xml:lang="en">4.21.12</label> sparśahānyāṃ hared raktaṃ
            pradihyānmadhurair api |
            <caesura/>
             kṣīrekṣurasasarpirbhiḥ secayec ca suśītalaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.21.13"><label xml:lang="en">4.21.13</label> piḍakām uttamākhyāṃ ca
            baḍiśenoddhared bhiṣak |
            <caesura/>
             uddhṛtya madhusaṃyuktaiḥ kaṣāyair avacūrṇayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.21.14"><label xml:lang="en">4.21.14</label> rasakriyā vidhātavyā likhite
            śataponake |
            <caesura/>
             pṛthak parṇyādisiddhaṃ ca deyaṃ tailam anantaram || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.21.15"><label xml:lang="en">4.21.15</label> kriyāṃ kuryād bhiṣak prājñas
            tvakpākasya visarpavat |
            <caesura/>
             raktavidradhivac cāpi kriyā śoṇitaje 'rbude || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.21.16"><label xml:lang="en">4.21.16</label> kaṣāyakalkasarpīṃṣi tailaṃ cūrṇaṃ
            rasakriyām |
            <caesura/>
             śodhanaṃ ropaṇaṃ caiva vīkṣya vīkṣyāvacārayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.21.17"><label xml:lang="en">4.21.17</label> hitaṃ ca sarpiṣaḥ pānaṃ pathyaṃ
            cāpi cirecanam |
            <caesura/>
             hitaḥ śoṇitamokṣaś ca yac cāpi laghu bhojanam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.21.18"><label xml:lang="en">4.21.18</label> arbudaṃ māṃsapākaṃ ca vidradhiṃ
            tilakālakam |
            <caesura/>
             pratyākhyāya prakurvīta bhiṣak samyak pratikriyām ||</l>

          <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ cikitsāsthāne śūkarogacikitsitaṃ
            nāmaikaviṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||21 ||</p>
        </div>


        <div n="22" type="adhyāya">
          <head>dvāviṃśatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>
          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.1"><label xml:lang="en">4.22.1</label> athāto mukharogacikitsitaṃ
            vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.2"><label xml:lang="en">4.22.2</label> yathovaca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.3"><label xml:lang="en">4.22.3</label> caturvidhena snehena
            madhūcchiṣṭayutena ca |
            <caesura/>
             vātaje 'bhyañjanaṃ dantavaidarbhe dantamūlāni śodhayet |
            <caesura/>
             tataḥ ksāraṃ prayuñjīta kriyāḥ sarvāś ca śītalāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.4"><label xml:lang="en">4.22.4</label> vidadhyādoṣṭhakope tu sālvaṇaṃ
            copanāhane| mastiṣke caiva nasye ca tailaṃ vātaharaṃ hitam|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.5"><label xml:lang="en">4.22.5</label> śrīveṣṭakaṃ sarjarasaṃ suradāru
            saguggulu| yaṣṭīmadhukacūrṇaṃ tu vidadhyāt pratisāraṇam|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.6"><label xml:lang="en">4.22.6</label> pittaraktābhighātotthaṃ jalaukobhir
            upācaret| pittavidradhivac cāpi kriyāṃ kuryād aśeṣataḥ|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.7"><label xml:lang="en">4.22.7</label> śirovirecanaṃ dhūmaḥ svedaḥ kavala
            eva ca| hṛte rakte prayoktavyamoṣṭhakope kaphātmake|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.8"><label xml:lang="en">4.22.8</label> tryūṣaṇaṃ svarjikākṣāro yavakṣāro
            viḍaṃ tathā| kṣaudrayuktaṃ vidhātavyametac ca pratisāraṇam|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.9"><label xml:lang="en">4.22.9</label> medoje svedite bhinne śodhite
            jvalano hitaḥ| priyaṅgutriphalālodhraṃ sakṣaudraṃ pratisāraṇam|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.10"><label xml:lang="en">4.22.10</label> etadoṣṭhaprakopānāṃ sādhyānāṃ
            karma kīrtitam| dantamūlagatānāṃ tu rogāṇāṃ karma vakṣyate|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.11"><label xml:lang="en">4.22.11</label> śītāde hṛtarakte tu toye
            nāgarasarṣapān| niṣkvāthya triphalāṃ mustaṃ gaṇḍūṣaḥ sarasāñjanaḥ|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.12"><label xml:lang="en">4.22.12</label> priyaṅgavaś ca mustaṃ ca triphalā
            ca pralepanam| nasyaṃ ca triphalāsiddhaṃ madhukotpalapadmakaiḥ|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.13"><label xml:lang="en">4.22.13</label> dantapuppuṭake kāryaṃ taruṇe
            raktamokṣaṇam| sapañcalavaṇaḥ kṣāraḥ sakṣaudraḥ pratisāraṇam|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.14"><label xml:lang="en">4.22.14</label> hitaḥ śirovirekaś ca nasyaṃ
            snigdhaṃ ca bhojanam| visrāvite dantaveṣṭe vraṇāṃs tu pratisārayet|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.15"><label xml:lang="en">4.22.15</label>
            rodhrapattaṅgayaṣṭyāhvalākṣācūrṇairmadhūttaraiḥ| gaṇḍūṣe kṣīriṇo yojyāḥ
            sakṣaudraghṛtaśarkarāḥ|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.16"><label xml:lang="en">4.22.16</label> kākolyādau daśakṣīrasiddhaṃ sarpiś
            ca nasyataḥ| śauṣire hṛtarakte tu rodhramustarasāñjanaiḥ|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.17"><label xml:lang="en">4.22.17</label> sakṣaudraiḥ śasyate lepo gaṇḍūṣe
            kṣīriṇo hitāḥ| sārivotpalayaṣṭyāhvasāvarāgurucandanaiḥ|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.18"><label xml:lang="en">4.22.18</label> kṣīre daśaguṇe siddhaṃ sarpirnasye
            ca pūjitam| kriyāṃ paridare kuyācchītākoktāṃ vicakṣaṇaḥ|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.19"><label xml:lang="en">4.22.19</label> saṃśodhyobhayataḥ kāryaṃ
            śiraścopakuśe tathā| kākodumbarikāgojīpatrairvisrāvayed asṛk|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.20"><label xml:lang="en">4.22.20</label> kṣaudrayuktaiś ca lavaṇaiḥ
            savyoṣaiḥ pratisārayet| pippalīḥ sarṣapāñ śvetānnāgaraṃ naiculaṃ phalam|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.21"><label xml:lang="en">4.22.21</label> sukhodakena saṃsṛjya kavalaṃ cāpi
            dhārayet| ghṛtaṃ madhurakaiḥ siddhaṃ hitaṃ kavalanasyayoḥ|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.22"><label xml:lang="en">4.22.22</label> śastreṇa dantavaidarbhe
            dantamūlāni śodhayet| tataḥ ksāraṃ prayuñjīta kriyāḥ sarvāś ca śītalāḥ|| </l>


          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.23"><label xml:lang="en">4.22.23</label> uddhṛtyādhikadantaṃ tu tato
            'gnimavacārayet |
            <caesura/>
             kṛmidantakavac cāpi vidhiḥ kāryo vijānatā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.24"><label xml:lang="en">4.22.24</label> chittvā 'dhimāṃsaṃ sakṣaudrair
            ebhiś cūrṇair upācaret |
            <caesura/>
             vacātejovatīpāṭhāsvarjikāyāvaśūkajaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.25"><label xml:lang="en">4.22.25</label> kṣaudradvitīyāḥ pippalyaḥ kavalaś
            cātra kīrtitaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             paṭolatriphalānimbakaṣāyaś cātra dhāvane |
            <caesura/>
             hitaḥ śirovirekaś ca dhūmo vair ecanaś ca yaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.26ab"><label xml:lang="en">4.22.26</label> sāmānyaṃ karma nāḍīnāṃ viśeṣaṃ
            cātra me śṛṇu |</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.26cd"> nāḍīvraṇaharaṃ karma dantanāḍīṣu kārayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.27"><label xml:lang="en">4.22.27</label> yaṃ dantam abhijāyeta nāḍī taṃ
            dantamuddharet |
            <caesura/>
             chittvā māṃsāni śastreṇa yadi noparijo bhavet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.28"><label xml:lang="en">4.22.28</label> śodhayitvā dahec cāpi kṣāreṇa
            jvalanena vā |
            <caesura/>
             bhinattyupekṣite dante hanukāsthi gatirdhruvam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.29"><label xml:lang="en">4.22.29</label> samūlaṃ daśanaṃ tasmād
            uddharedbhagnamasthiram |
            <caesura/>
             uddhṛte tūttare dante ca sthānaṃ vidahet suṣirasya ca |
            <caesura/>
             tato vidārīyaṣṭyāhvaśṛṅgāṭakakaserukaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.30"><label xml:lang="en">4.22.30</label> raktātiyogāt pūrvektā rogā ghorā
            bhavanti hi| kāṇaḥ saṃjāyate janturarditaṃ cāsya jāyate|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.31"><label xml:lang="en">4.22.31</label> calamapyuttaraṃ dantamato
            nāpaharedbhiṣak| dhāvane jātimadanasvādukaṇṭakakhādiram|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.32"><label xml:lang="en">4.22.32</label> kaṣāyaṃ
            jātimadanakaṭukasvādukaṇṭakaiḥ| yaṣṭyāhvarodhramañjiṣṭhākhadiraiś cāpi yat
            kṛtam|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.33"><label xml:lang="en">4.22.33</label> tailaṃ saṃśodhanaṃ taddhi hanyād
            dantagatāṃ gatim| kīrtitā dantamūle tu kriyā danteṣu vakṣyate|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.34"><label xml:lang="en">4.22.34</label> snehānāṃ kavalāḥ koṣṇāḥ
            sarpiṣastraivṛtasya vā| niryūhāś cānilaghnānāṃ dantaharṣapramardanāḥ|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.35"><label xml:lang="en">4.22.35</label> snaihikaś ca hito dhūmo nasyaṃ
            snigdhaṃ ca bhojanam| raso rasayavāgvaś ca kṣīraṃ santānikā ghṛtam|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.36"><label xml:lang="en">4.22.36</label> śirobastir hitaś cāpi kramo yaś
            cānilāpahaḥ| ahiṃsan dantamūlāni śarkarāmuddharedbhiṣak|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.37"><label xml:lang="en">4.22.37</label> lākṣācūrṇairmadhuyutais tatastāḥ
            pratisārayet| dantaharṣakriyāṃ cāpi kuryān niravaśeṣataḥ|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.38"><label xml:lang="en">4.22.38</label> kapālikā kṛcchratamā tatrāpy eṣā
            kriyā hitā| jayed visrāvaṇaiḥ svinnam acalaṃ kṛmidantakam|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.39"><label xml:lang="en">4.22.39</label> tathā+avapīḍair vātaghnaiḥ
            snehagaṇḍūṣadhāraṇaiḥ| bhadradārvādivarṣābhūlepaiḥ snigdhaiś ca bhojanaiḥ|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.40"><label xml:lang="en">4.22.40</label> calamuddhṛtya ca sthānaṃ vidahet
            suṣirasya ca| tato vidārīyaṣṭyāhvaśṛṅgāṭakakaserukaiḥ|| </l>


          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.41"><label xml:lang="en">4.22.41</label> tailaṃ daśaguṇe kṣīre siddhaṃ
            nasye hitaṃ bhavet |
            <caesura/>
             hanomokṣe samuddiṣṭāṃ kuryāc cārditavat kriyām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.42"><label xml:lang="en">4.22.42</label> phalānyamlāni śītāmbu rūkṣānnaṃ
            dantadhāvanam |
            <caesura/>
             tathā 'tikaṭhinān bhakṣyān dantarogī vivarjayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.43"><label xml:lang="en">4.22.43</label> sādhyānāṃ dantarogāṇāṃ
            cikitsitamudīritam |
            <caesura/>
             jihvāgatānāṃ sādhyānāṃ karma vakṣyāmi siddhaye || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.44"><label xml:lang="en">4.22.44</label> auṣṭhaprakope 'nilaje yaduktaṃ
            prāk cikitsitam |
            <caesura/>
             kaṇṭakeṣv anilottheṣu tat kāryaṃ bhiṣajā bhavet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.45"><label xml:lang="en">4.22.45</label> pittajeṣu vighṛṣṭeṣu niḥsṛte
            duṣṭaśoṇite |
            <caesura/>
             pratisāraṇagaṇḍūṣaṃ nasyaṃ ca madhuraṃ hitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.46"><label xml:lang="en">4.22.46</label> kaṇṭakeṣu kaphottheṣu likhiteṣv
            asṛjaḥ kṣaye |
            <caesura/>
             pippalyādirmadhuyutaḥ kāryas tu pratisāraṇe || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.47"><label xml:lang="en">4.22.47</label> gṛhṇīyāt kavalāṃś cāpi

        <div n="23" type="adhyāya">
          <head>trayoviṃśatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>
          <l xml:id="SS.4.23.1"><label xml:lang="en">4.23.1</label> athātaḥ śophānāṃ cikitsitaṃ
            vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.23.2"><label xml:lang="en">4.23.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.23.3"><label xml:lang="en">4.23.3</label> ṣaḍvidho 'vayavasamutthaḥ śopho
            'bhihito lakṣaṇataḥ pratīkārataś ca; sarvasaras tu pañcavidhaḥ, tad yathā
            vātapittaśleṣmasannipātaviṣanimittaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.23.4"><label xml:lang="en">4.23.4</label>
            tatrāpatarpitasyādhvagamanādatimātramabhyavaharato vā
            piṣṭānnaharitakaśākalavaṇāni kṣīṇasya vā 'timātramamlam upasevamānasya
            mṛtpakvaloṣṭakaṭaśarkarānūpaudakamāṃsasevanādajīrṇino vā
            grāmyadharmasevanādviruddhāhārasevanāt vā
            hastyaśvoṣṭrarathapadātisaṅkṣobhaṇādayo sitasya doṣā dhātūn pradūṣya śvayathum
            āpādayanty akhile śarīre || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.23.5"><label xml:lang="en">4.23.5</label> tatra vātaśvayathuraruṇaḥ kṛṣṇo vā
            mṛduranavasthitāstodādayaś cātra vedanāviśeṣāḥ; pittaśvayathuḥ pītaḥ sarakto
            vā mṛduḥ śīghrānusāryūṣādayaś cātra vedanāviśeṣāḥ; śleṣmaśvayathuḥ pāṇḍuḥ
            śuklo vā snigdhaḥ kaṭhinaḥ śīto mandānusārī, kaṇḍvādayaś cātra vedanāviśeṣāḥ;
            sannipātaśvayathuḥ sarvavarṇavedanaḥ; viṣanimittastu
            garopayogādduṣṭatoyasevanāt prakuthitodakāvagāhanāt
            saviṣasattvadigdhacūrṇāvacūrṇanādvā saviṣamūtrapurīṣaśukraspṛṣṭānāṃ vā
            tṛṇakāṣṭhādīnāṃ saṃsparśanāt, sa tu mṛduḥ ksiprotthāno 'valambī calo 'calo vā
            dāhapākarāgaprāyaś ca bhavati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.23.6"><label xml:lang="en">4.23.6</label> bhavanti cātra doṣāḥ
            śvayathumūrdhvaṃ hi kurvantyāmāśayasthitāḥ |
            <caesura/>
            <caesura/>
             pakvāśayasthā madhye ca varcaḥsthānagatāstvadhaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.23.7"><label xml:lang="en">4.23.7</label> kṛtsnaṃ dehamanuprāptāḥ kuryuḥ
            sarvasaraṃ tathā |
            <caesura/>
            <caesura/>
             śvayathur madhyadeśe yaḥ sa kaṣṭaḥ sarvagaś ca yaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.23.8"><label xml:lang="en">4.23.8</label> ardhāṅge 'riṣṭabhūtaś ca yaś
            cordhvaṃ parisarpati |
            <caesura/>
             śvāsaḥ pipāsā daurbalyaṃ jvaraś cchardirarocakaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.23.9"><label xml:lang="en">4.23.9</label> hikkātīsārakāsāś ca śūnaṃ
            saṅkṣapayanti hi |
            <caesura/>
             sāmānyato viśeṣāc ca teṣāṃ vakṣyāmi bheṣajam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.23.10"><label xml:lang="en">4.23.10</label> śophinaḥ sarva eva
            parihareyuramlalavaṇadadhiguḍavasāpayastailaghṛtapiṣṭamayagurūṇi || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.23.11"><label xml:lang="en">4.23.11</label> tatra vātaśvayathau
            traivṛtameraṇḍatailaṃ vā māsamardhamāsaṃ vā pāyayet,
            nyagrodhādikakaṣāyasiddhaṃ sarpiḥ pittaśvayathau, āragvadhādisiddhaṃ sarpiḥ
            śleṣmaśvayathau, sannipātaśvayathau snuhīkṣīrapātraṃ dvādaśabhir amlapātraiḥ
            pratisaṃsṛjya dantīdravantīpratīvāpaṃ sarpiḥ pācayitvā pāyayet, viṣanimitteṣu
            kalpeṣu pratīkāraḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.23.12"><label xml:lang="en">4.23.12</label> ata ūrdhvaṃ sāmānyacikitsitam
            upadekṣyāmaḥ tilvakaghṛtacaturthāni yānyuktānyudareṣu tato
            'nyataman upayujyamānaṃ śvayathumapahanti, mūtravartikriyāṃ vā seveta,
            navāyasaṃ vā 'haraharmadhunā,
            viḍaṅgātiviṣākuṭajaphalabhadradārunāgaramaricacūrṇaṃ vā dharaṇamuṣṇāmbunā,
            trikaṭukṣārāyaś cūrṇāni vā triphalākaṣāyeṇa, mūtraṃ vā tulyakṣīraṃ, harītakīṃ
            vā tulyaguḍām upayuñjīta, devadāruśuṇṭhīṃ vā, gugguluṃ vā mūtreṇa
            varṣabhūkaṣāyānupānaṃ vā, tulyaguḍaṃ vā mūtreṇa varṣabhūkaṣāyānupānaṃ vā,
            tulyaguḍaṃ śṛṅgaveraṃ vā, varṣābhūkaṣāyaṃ mūlakalkaṃ vā saśṛṅgaveraṃ payo
            'nupānam aharahar māsaṃ, vyoṣavarṣābhūkaṣāyasiddhena vā sarpiṣā mudgolumbān
            bhakṣayet, pippalīpippalīmūlacavyacitrakamayūrakavarṣābhūsiddhaṃ vā kṣīraṃ
            pibet, sahauṣadhamuraṅgīmūlasiddhaṃ vā, trikaṭukair aṇḍaśyāmāmūlasiddhaṃ vā,
            varṣābhūśṛṅgaverasahādevadārusiddhaṃ vā, tathā 'lābubibhītakaphalakalkaṃ vā
            taṇḍulāmbunā; kṣīrapippalīmaricaśṛṅgaverānusiddhena ca
            mudgayūṣeṇālavaṇenālpasnehena bhojayed yavānnaṃ godhūmānnaṃ vā;
            vṛkṣakārkanaktamālanimbavarṣābhūkvāthaiś ca pariṣekaḥ;
            sarṣapasuvarcalāsaindhavaśārṅgeṣṭābhiś ca pradehaḥ kāryaḥ; yathādoṣaṃ ca
            vamanavirecanāsthāpanāni tīkṣṇānyajasram upaseveta, snehasvedopanāhāṃś ca;
            sirābhiś cābhīkṣṇaṃ śoṇitam avasecayed anyatropadravaśophād iti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.23.13"><label xml:lang="en">4.23.13</label> bhavati cātra piṣṭānnam amlaṃ
            lavaṇāni madyaṃ mṛdaṃ divāsvapnam ajāṅgalaṃ ca |
            <caesura/>
             striyo ghṛtaṃ tailapayogurūṇi śophaṃ jighāṃsuḥ parivarjayet tu ||</l>

          <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ cikitsāsthāne sothacikitsitaṃ nāma
            trayoviṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||23 ||</p>
        </div>




        <div n="24" type="adhyāya">
          <head>caturviṃśatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>
          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.1"><label xml:lang="en">4.24.1</label> athāto 'nāgatābādhāpratiṣedhaṃ
            vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.2"><label xml:lang="en">4.24.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.3"><label xml:lang="en">4.24.3</label> utthāyotthāya satataṃ
            svasthenārogyam icchatā |
            <caesura/>
             dhīmatā yad anuṣṭheyaṃ tat sarvaṃ saṃpravakṣyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.4"><label xml:lang="en">4.24.4</label> tatrādau dantapavanaṃ
            dvādaśāṅgulamāyatam |
            <caesura/>
             kaniṣṭhikāparīṇāham ṛjvagranthitam avraṇam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.5"><label xml:lang="en">4.24.5</label> ayugmagranthi yac cāpi pratyagraṃ
            śastabhūmijam |
            <caesura/>
             avekṣyartuṃ ca doṣaṃ ca rasaṃ vīryaṃ ca yojayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.6"><label xml:lang="en">4.24.6</label> kaṣāyaṃ madhuraṃ tiktaṃ kaṭukaṃ
            prātar utthitaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             nimbaś ca tiktake śreṣṭhaḥ kaṣāye khadiras tathā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.7"><label xml:lang="en">4.24.7</label> madhūko madhure śreṣṭhaḥ karañjaḥ
            kaṭuke tathā |
            <caesura/>
             kṣaudravyoṣatrivargāktaṃ satailaṃ saindhavena ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.8"><label xml:lang="en">4.24.8</label> cūrṇena tejovatyāś ca dantān nityaṃ
            viśodhayet |
            <caesura/>
             ekaikaṃ ghrṣayed dantaṃ mṛdunā kūrcakena ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.9"><label xml:lang="en">4.24.9</label> dantaśodhanacūrṇena dantamāṃsāny
            abādhayan |
            <caesura/>
             tad daurgandhyopadehau tu śleṣmāṇaṃ cāpakarṣati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.10"><label xml:lang="en">4.24.10</label> vaiśadyam annābhir uciṃ
            saumanasyaṃ karoti ca |
            <caesura/>
             na khāded galatālv oṣṭhajihvārogasamudbhave || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.11"><label xml:lang="en">4.24.11</label> athāsyapāke śvāse ca
            kāsahikkāvamīṣu ca |
            <caesura/>
             durbalo 'jīrṇabhaktaś ca mūrcchārto madapīṣitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.12"><label xml:lang="en">4.24.12</label> śirorujārtastṛṣitaḥ śrāntaḥ
            pānaklamānvitaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             arditī karṇaśūlī ca dantarogī ca mānavaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.13"><label xml:lang="en">4.24.13</label> jihvānirlekhanaṃ raupyaṃ sauvarṇaṃ
            vārkṣam eva ca |
            <caesura/>
             tan malāpaharaṃ śastaṃ mṛdu ślakṣṇaṃ daśāṅgulam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.14"><label xml:lang="en">4.24.14</label> mukhavair asya
            daurgandhyaśophajāḍyaharaṃ sukham |

            narendradviṣṭonmattapatitakṣudranīcān upāsīta || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.91"><label xml:lang="en">4.24.91</label>
            vṛkṣaparvataprapātaviṣamavalmīkaduṣṭavājikuñjarādyadhirohaṇāni pariharet,
            pūrṇanadīsamudrāviditapalvalaśvabhrakūpāvataraṇāni,
            bhinnaśūnyāgāraśmaśānavijanāraṇyavāsāgnisaṃbhramavyālabhujaṅgakīṭasevāś ca,
            grāmāghātakalahaśastrasannipātavyālasarīsṛpaśṛṅgisannikarṣāṃś ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.92"><label xml:lang="en">4.24.92</label>
            nāgnigogurubrāhmaṇapreṅkhādampatyantareṇa yāyāt | na śavam anuyāyāt |
            devagobrāhmaṇacaity adhvajarogipatitapāpakāriṇāṃ ca chāyāṃ nākrameta | nāstaṃ
            gacchantam udyantaṃ vā ''ādity aṃ vīkṣeta | gāṃ dhāpayantīṃ dhayantīṃ
            paraśasyaṃ vā carantīṃ na kasmaicid ācakṣīta, na colkāpātotpātendradhanūṃṣi |
            nāgniṃ mukhenopadhamet | nāpo bhūmiṃ vā pāṇipādenābhihanyāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.93"><label xml:lang="en">4.24.93</label> na vegān dhārayed
            vātamūtrapurīṣādīnām | na bahirvegān
            grāmanagaradevatāyatanaśmaśānacatuṣpathasalilāśayapathisannikṛṣṭāv utsṛjen na
            prakāśaṃ na vāyvagnisalilasomārkagogurupratimukham || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.94"><label xml:lang="en">4.24.94</label> na bhūmiṃ vilikhet,
            nāsaṃvṛtamukhaḥ sadasi jṛmbhodagārakāsaśvāsakṣavathūnutsṛjet, na
            paryaṅkikāvaṣṭambhapādaprasāraṇāni gurusannidhau kuryāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.95"><label xml:lang="en">4.24.95</label> na
            bālakarṇanāsāsrotodaśanākṣivivarāṇyabhikuṣṇīyāt, na vījayet
            keśamukhanakhavastragātrāṇi, na gātranakhavaktravāditraṃ kuryāt , na
            kāṣṭhaloṣṭatṛṇādīn abhihanyāc chindyād bhindyād vā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.96"><label xml:lang="en">4.24.96</label> na prativātātapaṃ seveta, na
            bhuktamātro 'gnimupāsīta, notkaṭakālpakāṣṭhāsanamadhyāsīta, na grīvāṃ viṣamaṃ
            dhārayet, na viṣamakāyaḥ kriyāṃ bhajeta bhuñjīta vā, na pratatam īkṣeta
            viśeṣājjyotirbhāskarasūkṣmacalabhrāntāni, na bhāraṃ śirasā vahet, na
            svapnajāgaraṇaśayanāsanasthānacaṅkramaṇayānavāhanapradhāvanalaṅghanaplavanaprataraṇahāsyabhāṣyavyavāyavyāyāmādīnucitān
            apy atiseveta || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.97"><label xml:lang="en">4.24.97</label> ucitād apy ahitāt kramaśo viramet,
            hitam anucitam apy aseveta kramaśaḥ, na caikāntataḥ pādahīnāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.98"><label xml:lang="en">4.24.98</label> nāvākśirāḥ śayīta, na bhinnapātre
            bhuñjīta, na vinā pātreṇa, nāñjalipuṭenāpaḥ pibet, kāle
            hitamitasnigdhamadhuraprāyamāhāraṃ vaidyapratyavekṣitam aśnīyāt,
            grāmagaṇagaṇikāpaṇikaśatrusatraśaṭhapatitabhojanāni parikaret, śeṣāṇy api
            cāniṣṭarūparasagandhasparśaśabdamānasāni, anyāny evaṃ guṇāny api
            saṃbhramadattāni, (tānyapi) makṣikābālopahatāni, nāprakṣālitapādo bhuñjīta na
            mūtroccārapīḍito na sandhyayor nānupāśrito nātītakālaṃ hīnam atimātraṃ
            (noddhṛtasnehaṃ) ceti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.99"><label xml:lang="en">4.24.99</label> na bhuñjītoddhṛtasnehaṃ naṣṭaṃ
            paryuṣitaṃ payaḥ | na naktaṃ dadhi bhuñjīta na cāpy aghṛtaśarkaram || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.100"><label xml:lang="en">4.24.100</label> nāmudgayūṣaṃ nākṣaudraṃ noṣṇaṃ
            nāmalakair vinā | anyathā janayet kuṣṭhavisarpādīn gadān bahūn | nātmānamudake
            paśyen na nagnaḥ praviśejjalam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.101"><label xml:lang="en">4.24.101</label>
            dyūtamadyātisevāpratibhutvasākṣitvasamāhvānagoṣṭhīvāditrāṇi na seveta, srajaṃ
            chatropānakau kanakam atītavāsāṃsi na cānyair dhṛtāni dhārayet, brāhmaṇam
            agniṃ gāṃ ca nocchiṣṭaḥ spṛśet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.102"><label xml:lang="en">4.24.102</label> bhavanti cātra yasmin yasminn
            ṛtau ye ye doṣāḥ kupyanti dehinām |
            <caesura/>
             teṣu teṣu pradātavyā rasāste te vijānatā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.103"><label xml:lang="en">4.24.103</label> varṣāsu na pibet toyaṃ pibec
            charadi mātrayā |
            <caesura/>
             varṣasu caturo māsān mātrāvad udakaṃ pibet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.104"><label xml:lang="en">4.24.104</label> uṣṇaṃ haime vasante ca kāmaṃ
            śrīṣme tu śītalam |
            <caesura/>
             hemante ca vasante ca sīdhvariṣṭau piben naraḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.105"><label xml:lang="en">4.24.105</label> śṛtaśītaṃ payo grīṣme prāvṛṭkāle
            rasaṃ pibet |
            <caesura/>
             yūṣaṃ varṣati, tasyānte prapicchītalaṃ jalam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.106"><label xml:lang="en">4.24.106</label> svastha evam ato 'nyas tu
            doṣāhāragatānugaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             snehaṃ saindhavacūrṇena pippalībhiś ca saṃyutam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.107"><label xml:lang="en">4.24.107</label> pibed agnivivṛddhyarthaṃ na ca
            vegān vidhārayet |
            <caesura/>
             agnidīptikaraṃ nṝṇāṃ rogāṇāṃ śamanaṃ prati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.108"><label xml:lang="en">4.24.108</label> prāvṛṭśaradvasanteṣu samyak
            snehādimācaret |
            <caesura/>
             kaphe pracchardanaṃ pitte vireko bastirīrane || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.109"><label xml:lang="en">4.24.109</label> śasyate triṣv api sadā vyāyāmo
            doṣanāśanaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             bhuktaṃ viruddham apy annaṃ vyāyāmānna praduṣyati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.110"><label xml:lang="en">4.24.110</label> utsargamaithunahāraśodhane syāt
            tu tanmanāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             necched doṣacayāt prājñaḥ pīḍāṃ vā kāyamānasīm || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.111"><label xml:lang="en">4.24.111</label> atistrīsaṃprayogāc ca rakṣed
            ātmānam ātmavān |
            <caesura/>
             śūlakāsajvaraśvāsakārśyapāṇḍvāmayakṣayāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.112"><label xml:lang="en">4.24.112</label> ativyavājāj jāyante rogāś
            cākṣepakādayaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             āyuṣmanto mandajarā vapur varṇabalānvitāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.113"><label xml:lang="en">4.24.113</label> sthiropacitamāṃsāś ca bhavanti
            strīṣu saṃyatāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             tribhis tribhir ahobhir vā samīyāt pramadāṃ naraḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.114"><label xml:lang="en">4.24.114</label> sarveṣvṛtuṣu, gharmeṣu pakṣāt
            pakṣād vrajed budhaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             rajasvalām akāmāṃ ca malinām apriyāṃ tathā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.115"><label xml:lang="en">4.24.115</label> varṇavṛddhāṃ vayovṛddhāṃ tathā
            vyādhiprapīḍitām |
            <caesura/>
             hīnāṅgīṃ garbhiṇīṃ dveṣyāṃ yonidoṣasamanvitām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.116"><label xml:lang="en">4.24.116</label> sagotrāṃ gurupatnīṃ ca tathā
            pravrajitām api |
            <caesura/>
             sandhyāparvasvagamyāṃ ca nopeyāt pramadāṃ naraḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.117"><label xml:lang="en">4.24.117</label> gosarge cārdharātre ca tathā
            madhyandineṣu ca |
            <caesura/>
             lajjāsamāvahe deśe vivṛte 'śuddha eva ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.118"><label xml:lang="en">4.24.118</label> kṣudhito vyādhitaś caiva
            kṣubdhacittaś ca mānavaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             vātaviṇmūtravegī ca pipāsaratidurbalaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.119"><label xml:lang="en">4.24.119</label> tiryagyonāv ayonau ca
            prāptaśukravidhāraṇam |
            <caesura/>
             duṣṭayonau visargaṃ tu balavān api varjayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.120"><label xml:lang="en">4.24.120</label> retasaś cātimātraṃ tu
            mūrdhāvaraṇam eva ca |
            <caesura/>
             sthitāvuttānaśayane viśeṣeṇaiva garhitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.121"><label xml:lang="en">4.24.121</label> krīḍāyām api medhāvī hitārthī
            parivarjayet |
            <caesura/>
             rajasvalāṃ prāptavato narasyāniyatātmanaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.122"><label xml:lang="en">4.24.122</label> dṛṣṭyāyustejasāṃ hānir adharmaś
            ca tato bhavet |
            <caesura/>
             liṅginīṃ gurupatnīṃ ca sagotrām atha parvasu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.123"><label xml:lang="en">4.24.123</label> vṛddhāṃ ca sandhyayoś cāpi
            gacchato jīvitakṣayaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             garbhiṇyā garbhapīḍā syād vyādhitāyāṃ balakṣayaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.124"><label xml:lang="en">4.24.124</label> hīnāṅgīṃ malināṃ dveṣyāṃ kāmaṃ
            vandhyāmasaṃvṛte |
            <caesura/>
             deśe 'śuddhe ca śukrasya manasaś ca kṣayo bhavet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.125"><label xml:lang="en">4.24.125</label> kṣudhitaḥ kṣubdhacittaś ca
            madhyāhne tṛṣito 'balaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             sthitaś ca hāniṃ śukrasya vāyoḥ kopaṃ ca vindati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.126"><label xml:lang="en">4.24.126</label> atiprasaṅgād bhavati śoṣaḥ
            śukrakṣayāvahaḥ | vyādhitasya rujā plīhni mṛtyur mūrcchā ca jāyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.127"><label xml:lang="en">4.24.127</label> prayūṣasy ardharātre ca
            vātapitte prakupyataḥ |
            <caesura/>
             tiryagyonāv ayanau ca duṣṭayonau tathaiva ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.128"><label xml:lang="en">4.24.128</label> upadaṃśas tathā vāyoḥ kopaḥ
            śukrasya ca kṣayaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             uccārite mūtrite ca retasaś ca vidhāraṇe || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.129"><label xml:lang="en">4.24.129</label> uttāne ca bhavec chīghraṃ
            śukrāśmaryās tu saṃbhavaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             sarvaṃ pariharet tasmād etal lokadvaye 'hitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.130"><label xml:lang="en">4.24.130</label> śukraṃ copasthitaṃ mohānna
            sandhāryaṃ kathaṃcana |
            <caesura/>
             vayor ūpaguṇopetāṃ tulyaśīlāṃ kulānvitām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.131"><label xml:lang="en">4.24.131</label> abhikāmo 'bhikāmāṃ tu hṛṣṭo
            hṛṣṭām alaṅkṛtām |
            <caesura/>
             seveta pramadāṃ yuktyā vājīkaraṇabṛṃhitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.132"><label xml:lang="en">4.24.132</label> bhakṣyāḥ saśarkarāḥ kṣīraṃ
            sasitaṃ rasa eva ca |
            <caesura/>
             snānaṃ savyajanaṃ svapno vyavāyānte hitāni tu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.133"><label xml:lang="en">4.24.133</label> mukhamātraṃ samāsena
            sadvṛttasyaitad īritam |
            <caesura/>
             ārogyam āyur artho vāg āsadbhiḥ prāpyate nṛbhiḥ ||</l>

            caturviṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||24 ||</p>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.25.25"><label xml:lang="en">4.25.25</label> lopākānūpamajjānaṃ vasāṃ tailaṃ

            <caesura/>
             paceddaśaguṇaṃ kṣīramāvāpya madhuraṃ gaṇam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.25.26"><label xml:lang="en">4.25.26</label> apāmārgāśvagandhe ca tathā
            lākṣārasaṃ śubham |
            <caesura/>
             tatsiddhaṃ paripūtaṃ ca svanuguptaṃ nidhāpayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.25.27"><label xml:lang="en">4.25.27</label> tenābhyañjyāt sadā pālīṃ
            susvinnāmtimarditām |
            <caesura/>
             etena pālyo vardhante nirujo nirupadravāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.25.28"><label xml:lang="en">4.25.28</label> mṛdvyaḥ puṣṭāḥ samāḥ snigdhā
            jāyante bhūṣaṇakṣamāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             nīlīdalaṃ bhṛṅgarajo 'rjunatvak piṇḍītakaṃ kṛṣṇamayor ajaś ca |
            <caesura/>
             bījodbhavaṃ sāhacaraṃ ca puṣpaṃ pathyākṣadhātrīsahitaṃ vicūrṇya || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.25.29"><label xml:lang="en">4.25.29</label> ekīkṛtaṃ sarvam idaṃ pramāya
            paṅkena tulyaṃ nalinībhavena |
            <caesura/>
             saṃyojya pakṣaṃ kalaśe nidhāya lauhe vipacedvimiśraṃ rasena
            bhṛṅgatriphalābhavena |
            <caesura/>
             āsannapāke ca parīkṣaṇārthaṃ patraṃ balākābhavam ākṣipec ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.25.30"><label xml:lang="en">4.25.30</label> anena tailaṃ vipaced vimiśraṃ
            rasena bhṛṅgatriphalābhavena| āsannapāke ca parīkṣaṇārthaṃ patraṃ
            balākābhavamākṣipecca|| </l>


          <l xml:id="SS.4.25.31"><label xml:lang="en">4.25.31</label> bhaved yadā tadbhramarāṅganīlaṃ
            tadā vipakvaṃ vinidhāya pātre |
            <caesura/>
             kṛṣṇāyase māsam avasthitaṃ tadabhyaṅgayogāt palitāni hanyāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.25.32"><label xml:lang="en">4.25.32</label> sairīyajambvarjunakāśmarījaṃ
            puṣpaṃ tilānmārkavacūtabīje |
            <caesura/>
             punarnave kardamakaṇṭakāryau kāsīsapiṇḍītakabījasāram || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.25.33"><label xml:lang="en">4.25.33</label> phalatrayaṃ loharajo 'ñjanaṃ ca
            yaṣṭyāhvayaṃ nīrajasārive ca |
            <caesura/>
             piṣṭvā 'tha sarvaṃ saha modayanty ā sārāmbhasā bījakasaṃbhavena || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.25.34"><label xml:lang="en">4.25.34</label> sārāmbhasaḥ saptabhir eva paś cāt
            prasthaiḥ samāloḍya daśāhaguptam |
            <caesura/>
             lauhe supātre vinidhāya tailamakṣodbhavaṃ tac ca pacet prayatnāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.25.35"><label xml:lang="en">4.25.35</label> pakvaṃ ca lauhe 'bhinave nidhāya
            nasyaṃ vidadhyāt pariśuddhakāyaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             abhyaṅgayogaiś ca niyujyamānaṃ bhuñjīta māṣān kṛśarāmatho vā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.25.36"><label xml:lang="en">4.25.36</label> māsopariṣṭād ghanakuñjitāgrāḥ keśā
            bhavanti bhramarāñjanābhāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             keśās tathā 'nye khalatau bhaveyurjarā na cainaṃ sahasā 'bhyupaiti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.25.37"><label xml:lang="en">4.25.37</label> balaṃ paraṃ saṃbhavatīndiryāṇāṃ
            bhavec ca vaktraṃ valibhir vimuktam |
            <caesura/>
             nākāmine 'nārthini nākṛtāya naivāraye tailamidaṃ pradeyam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.25.38"><label xml:lang="en">4.25.38</label> lākṣā rodhraṃ dve haridre śilāle
            kuṣṭhaṃ nāgaṃ gair ikā varṇakāś ca |
            <caesura/>
             mañjiṣṭhogrā syāt surāṣṭrodbhavā ca pattaṅgaṃ vai rocanā cāñjanaṃ ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.25.39"><label xml:lang="en">4.25.39</label> hemāṅgatvak pāṇḍupatraṃ vaṭasya
            kālīyaṃ syāt padmakaṃ padmamadhyam |
            <caesura/>
             raktaṃ śvetaṃ candanaṃ pāradaṃ ca kākolyādiḥ kṣīrapiṣṭaś ca vargaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.25.40"><label xml:lang="en">4.25.40</label> medo majjā sikthakaṃ goghṛtaṃ ca
            dugdhaṃ kvāthaḥ kṣīriṇāṃ ca drumāṇām |
            <caesura/>
             etat sarvaṃ pakvam aikadhyatas tu vaktrābhyaṅge sarpir uktaṃ pradhānam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.25.41"><label xml:lang="en">4.25.41</label> hanyād vyaṅgaṃ nīlikāṃ cātivṛddhāṃ
            vaktre jātāḥ sphoṭikāś cāpi kāś cit |
            <caesura/>
             padmākāraṃ nirvalīkaṃ ca vaktraṃ kuryād etat pīnagaṇḍaṃ manojñam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.25.42"><label xml:lang="en">4.25.42</label> rājñām etad yoṣitāṃ cāpi nityaṃ
            kuryād vaidyas tat samānāṃ nṛṇāṃ ca |
            <caesura/>
             kuṣṭhaghnaṃ vai sarpiretat pradhānaṃ yeṣāṃ pāde santi vaipādikāś ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.25.43"><label xml:lang="en">4.25.43</label> harīkakīcūrṇamariṣṭapatraṃ
            cūtatvacaṃ dāḍimapuṣpavṛntam |
            <caesura/>
             patraṃ ca dadyān madayantikāyā lepo 'ṅgarāgo naradevayogyaḥ ||</l>

          <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ cikitsāsthāne miśrakacikitsitaṃ nāma
            pañcaviṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||25 ||</p>

        <div n="27" type="adhyāya">
          <head>saptaviṃśatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>
          <l xml:id="SS.4.27.1"><label xml:lang="en">4.27.1</label> athātaḥ sarvopaghātaśamanīyaṃ
            rasāyanaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.27.2"><label xml:lang="en">4.27.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.27.3"><label xml:lang="en">4.27.3</label> pūrve vayasi madhye vā manuṣyasya
            rasāyanam |
            <caesura/>
             prayuñjīta bhiṣak prājñaḥ snigdhaśuddhatanoḥ sadā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.27.4"><label xml:lang="en">4.27.4</label> nāviśuddhaśarīrasya yukto rāsāyano
            vidhiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             na bhāti vāsasi kliṣṭe raṅgayoga ivāhitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.27.5"><label xml:lang="en">4.27.5</label> śarīrasyopaghātā ye doṣajā mānasās
            tathā |
            <caesura/>
             upadiṣṭāḥ pradeśeṣu teṣāṃ vakṣyāmi vāraṇam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.27.6"><label xml:lang="en">4.27.6</label> śītodakaṃ payaḥ kṣaudraṃ sarpirity
            ekaśo dviśaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             triśaḥ samastamathavā prāk pītaṃ sthāpayed vayaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.27.7"><label xml:lang="en">4.27.7</label> tatra viḍaṅgataṇḍulacūrṇamāhṛtya
            yaṣṭīmadhukamadhuyuktaṃ yathābalaṃ śītatoyenopayuñjīta śītatoyaṃ cānupibed
            evam aharahar māsaṃ, tad eva madhuyuktaṃ bhallātakakvāthena vā,
            madhudrākṣākvāthayuktaṃ vā, madhvāmalakarasābhyāṃ vā, guḍūcīkvāthena vā, evam
            ete pañca prayogā bhavanti; jīrṇe mudgāmalakayūṣeṇālavaṇenālpasnehena
            ghṛtavantam odanam aśnīyāt; ete svalvarśāṃsi kṣapayanti, kṛmīn upaghnanti,
            grahaṇadhāraṇaśaktiṃ janayanti, māse māse ca prayoge varṣaśataṃ
            varṣaśatamāyuṣo 'bhivṛddhir bhavati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.27.8"><label xml:lang="en">4.27.8</label> viḍaṅgataṇḍulānāṃ droṇaṃ piṣṭapacane
            piṣṭavadupasvedya vigatakaṣāyaṃ svinnamavatārya dṛṣadi piṣṭamāyase dṛḍhe
            kumbhe madhūdakottaraṃ prāvṛṣi bhasmarāśāvantargṛhe caturo māsānnidadhyāt,
            varṣāvigame coddhṛtyopasaṃskṛtaśarīraḥ sahasrasaṃpātābhihutaṃ kṛtvā
            prātaḥprātar yathābalam upayuñjīta, jīrṇe mudgāmalakayūṣeṇālavaṇena
            ghṛtavantam odanam aśnīyāt, pāṃśuśayyāyāṃ śayīta, tasya māsādūrdhvaṃ
            sarvāṅgebhyaḥ kṛmayo niṣkrāmanti, tān aṇutailenābhyaktasya
            vaṃśavidalenāpaharet, dvitīye pipīlikāstṛtīye yūkāstathaivāpaharet, caturthe
            dantanakharomāṇyavaśīryante; pañcame praśastaguṇalakṣaṇāni jāyante, amānuṣaṃ
            cādity aprakāśaṃ vapuradhigacchati, dūrācchravaṇāni darśanā nicāsya bhavanti,
            rajastamasī cāpohya sattvam adhitiṣṭhati, śrutanigādyapūrvotpādī gajabalo
            'śvajavaḥ punaryuvā 'ṣṭau varṣaśatānyāyuravāpnoti; tasyāṇutailamabhyaṅgārthe,
            candanam upalepanārthe, bhallātakavidhānavadāhāraḥ parihāraś ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.27.9"><label xml:lang="en">4.27.9</label> kāśmaryāṇāṃ niṣkulīkṛtānāmeṣa eva
            kalpaḥ pāṃśuśayyābhojanavarjaṃ; atra hi payasā śṛtena bhoktavyaṃ, samānamanyat
            pūrveṇāśiṣaś ca | śoṇitapittanimitteṣu vikāreṣveteṣām upayogaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.27.10"><label xml:lang="en">4.27.10</label> yathoktamāgāraṃ praviśya
            balāmūlārdhapalaṃ palaṃ vā payasā ''āloḍya pibet, jīrṇe payaḥ sarpirodana ity
            āhāraḥ, evaṃ dvādaśarātram upayujya dvādaśa varṣāṇi vayastiṣṭhati; evaṃ
            divasaśatam upayujya varṣaśataṃ vayastiṣṭhati | evam
            evātibalānāgabalāvidārīśatāvarīṇām upayogaḥ | viśeṣatastvatibalāmudakena,
            nāgabalācūrṇaṃ madhunā, vidārīcūrṇaṃ kṣīreṇa, śatāvarīmapyevaṃ, pūrveṇānyat
            samānamāśiṣaś ca samāḥ | etāstvauṣadhayo balakāmānāṃ śoṣiṇāṃ
            raktapittopasṛṣṭānāṃ śoṇitaṃ chardayatāṃ viricyamānānāṃ copadiśyante || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.27.11"><label xml:lang="en">4.27.11</label> vārāhīmūlatulācūrṇaṃ kṛtvā tato
            mātrāṃ madhuyuktāṃ payasā ''āloḍya pibet, jīrṇe payaḥ sarpirodana ity āhāraḥ,
            pratibedho 'tra pūrvavat; prayogamimam upasevamāno varṣaśatamāyuravāpnoti
            strīṣu cākṣayatām, etenaiva cūrṇena payo 'vacūrṇya śṛtaśītam
            abhimathyājyamutpādya madhuyutam upayuñjīta sāyaṃprātar ekakālaṃ vā, jīrṇe
            payaḥ sarpirodana ity āhāraḥ, evaṃ māsam upayujya sauparṇaṃ bhavaty analpabalaḥ
            strīṣu cākṣayo varṣaśatāyurbhavatīti || </l>


          <l xml:id="SS.4.27.12"><label xml:lang="en">4.27.12</label> cakṣuḥkāmaḥ prāṇakāmo vā
            bījakasārāgnimanthamūlaṃ niṣkvāthya māṣaprasthaṃ sādhayet, tasmin sidhyati
            citrakamūlānām akṣamātraṃ kalkaṃ dadyād āmalakarasacaturthabhāgaṃ, tataḥ
            svinnam avatārya sahasrasṃpātābhihutaṃ kṛtvā śītībhūtaṃ madhusarpirbhyāṃ
            saṃsṛjyopayuñjīta yathābalaṃ, yathāsātmyaṃ ca lavaṇaṃ pariharan bhakṣayet|
            jīrṇe mudgāmalakayūṣeṇālavaṇena ghṛtavantamodanamaśnīyāt payasā vā māsatrayam;
            evamābhyāṃ prayogābhyāṃ cakṣuḥ sauparṇaṃ bhavaty analpabalaḥ strīṣu cākṣayo
            varṣaśatāyur bhavatīti|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.27.13"><label xml:lang="en">4.27.13</label> bhavati cātra payasā saha siddhāni
            naraḥ śaṇaphalāni yaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             bhakṣayet payasā sārdhaṃ vayas tasya na śīryate ||</l>

          <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ cikitsāsthāne sarvopaghātaśamanīyaṃ
            rasāyanacikitsitaṃ nāma saptaviṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||27 ||</p>
        </div>


        <div n="28" type="adhyāya">
          <head>aṣṭaviṃśatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>
          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.1"><label xml:lang="en">4.28.1</label> athāto medhāyuṣkāmīyaṃ
            rasāyanacikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.2"><label xml:lang="en">4.28.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvanatariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.3"><label xml:lang="en">4.28.3</label> medhāyuḥkāmaḥ
            śvetāvalgujaphalānyātapapariśuṣkāṇyādāya sūkṣmacūrṇāni kṛtvā guḍena sahāloḍya
            snehakumbhe saptarātraṃ dhānyarāśau nidadhyāt, saptarātrād uddhṛtya
            hṛtadoṣasya yathābalaṃ piṇḍaṃ prayacched anudite sūrye, uṣṇodakaṃ cānupibet;
            bhallātakavidhānavac cāgārapraveśaḥ, jīrṇauṣadhaś cāparāhṇe himābhir adbhiḥ
            pariṣiktagātraḥ śālīnāṃ ṣaṣṭikānāṃ ca payasā śarkarāmadhureṇaudanam aśnīyāt;
            evaṃ ṣaṇmāsān upayujya vigatapāpmā balavarṇopetaḥ śrutanigādī smṛtimān arogo
            varṣaśatāyur bhavati | kuṣṭhinaṃ pāṇḍurogiṇam udariṇaṃ vā kṛṣṇāyā
            gomūtreṇāloḍyārdhapalikaṃ piṇḍaṃ vigatalauhitye savitari pāyayet, parāhṇe
            cālavaṇenāmalakayūṣeṇa sarpiṣmantam odanam aśnīyāt, evaṃ māsam upayujya
            smṛtimān arogo varṣaśatāyur bhavati | eṣa evopayogaś citrakamūlānāṃ rajanyāś
            ca; citrakamūle viśeṣo dvipalikaṃ piṇḍaṃ paraṃ pramāṇaṃ, śeṣaṃ pūrvavat || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.4"><label xml:lang="en">4.28.4</label> hṛtadoṣa eva pratisaṃsṛṣṭabhakto
            yathākramamāgāraṃ praviśya maṇḍūkaparṇīsvarasam ādāya sahasrasaṃpātābhihutaṃ
            kṛtvā yathābalaṃ payasā ''āloḍya pibet payo 'nupānaṃ vā, tasyāṃ jīrṇāyāṃ
            yavānnaṃ payasopayuñjīta; tilair vā saha bhakṣayet trīn māsān payo 'nupānaṃ,
            jīrṇe payaḥ sarpirodana ity āhāraḥ; evam upayuñjāno brahmavarcasī śrutanigādī
            bhavati varṣaśatam āyur avāpnoti | trirātropoṣitaś ca trirātram enāṃ
            bhakṣayet, trirātrādūrdhvaṃ payaḥ sarpir iti copayuñjīta | bilvamātraṃ piṇḍaṃ
            vā payasā ''āloḍya pibet, evaṃ dvādaśarātram upayujya medhāvī varṣaśatāyur
            bhavati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.5"><label xml:lang="en">4.28.5</label> hṛtadoṣa evāgāraṃ praviśya
            pratisaṃsṛṣṭabhakto brāhmīsvarasamādāya sahasrasaṃpātābhihutaṃ kṛtvā
            yathābalampayuñjīta, jīrṇauṣadhaś cāparāhṇe yavāgūmalavaṇaṃ pibet, kṣīrasātmyo
            vā payasā bhuñjīta, evaṃ saptarātram upayujya brahmavarcasī medhāvī bhavati,
            dvitīyaṃ saptarātram upayujya grantham īpsitam utpādayati naṣṭaṃ cāsya prādur
            bhavati, tṛtīyaṃ saptarātram upayujya dviruccāritaṃ śatam apy avadhārayati,
            evam ekaviṃśatirātram upayujyālakṣmīr apakrāmati; mūrtimatī cainaṃ vāgdevy
            anupraviśati, sarvāś cainaṃ śrutaya upatiṣṭhanti, śrutadharaḥ
            pañcavarṣaśatāyur bhavati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.6"><label xml:lang="en">4.28.6</label> brāhmīsvarasaprasthadvaye
            ghṛtaprasthaṃ viḍaṅgataṇḍulānāṃ kuḍavaṃ dve dve pale vacāmṛtayor dvādaśa
            harītakyāmalakabibhītakāni ślakṣṇapiṣṭānyāvāpyaikadhyaṃ sādhayitvā svanuguptaṃ
            nidadhyāt, tataḥ pūrvavidhānena mātrāṃ yathābalam upayuñjīta, jīrṇe payaḥ
            sarpirodana ity āhāraḥ, pūrvavac cātra parīhāraḥ, etenordhvam adhas tiryak
            kṛmayo niṣkrāmanti, alakṣmīr apakrāmati, puṣkaravarṇaḥ sthiravayāḥ śrutanigādī
            trivarṣaśatāyur bhavati; etad eva
            kuṣṭhaviṣamajvarāpasmāronmādaviṣabhūtagraheṣv anyeṣu ca mahāvyādhiṣu
            saṃśodhanam ādiśanti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.7"><label xml:lang="en">4.28.7</label> hṛtadoṣa evāgāraṃ praviśya
            haimavatyā vacāyāḥ piṇḍamāmalakamātram abhihutaṃ payasā ''āloḍya pibet, jīrṇe
            payaḥ sarpirodana ity āhāraḥ, evaṃ dvādaśarātram upayuñjīta, tato 'sya śrotraṃ
            vivriyate, dvirabhyāsāt smṛtimān bhavati, trirabhyāsācchrutamādatte,
            caturdvādaśarātram upayujya sarvaṃ tarati kilbiṣaṃ, tārkṣyadarśanamutpadyate,
            śatāyuś ca bhavati | dve dve pale itarasyā vacāyā viṣkvāthya pibet payasā,
            samānaṃ bhojanaṃ, samāḥ pūrveṇāśiṣaś ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.8"><label xml:lang="en">4.28.8</label> vacāśatapākaṃ vā sarpirdroṇam
            upayujya pañcavarṣaśatāyurbhavati, galagaṇḍāpacīślīpadasvaramedāṃś cāpahantīti
            || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.9"><label xml:lang="en">4.28.9</label> ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi
            āyuṣkāmarasāyanam |
            <caesura/>
             mantrauṣadhasamāyuktaṃ saṃvatsaraphalapradam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.10"><label xml:lang="en">4.28.10</label> bilvasya cūrṇaṃ puṣye tu hutaṃ
            vārān sahasraśaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             śrīsūktena naraḥ kalye sasuvarṇaṃ dine dine || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.11"><label xml:lang="en">4.28.11</label> sarpir madhuyutaṃ
            lihyād alakṣmīnāśanaṃ param |
            <caesura/>
             tvacaṃ vihāya bilvasya mūlakvāthaṃ dine dine || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.12"><label xml:lang="en">4.28.12</label> prāśnīyāt payasā sārdhaṃ snātvā
            hutvā samāhitaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             daśasāhasram āyuṣyaṃ smṛtaṃ yuktarathaṃ bhavet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.13"><label xml:lang="en">4.28.13</label> hutvā bisānāṃ kvāthaṃ tu
            madhulājaiś ca saṃyutam |
            <caesura/>
             amoghaṃ śatasāhasraṃ yuktaṃ yuktarathaṃ smṛtam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.14"><label xml:lang="en">4.28.14</label> suvarṇaṃ padmabījāni madhu lājāḥ
            priyaṅgavaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             gavyena payasā pītam alakṣmīṃ pratiṣedhayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.15"><label xml:lang="en">4.28.15</label> nīlotpaladalakvātho gavyena payasā
            śṛtaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             sasuvarṇastilaiḥ sārdham alakṣmīnāśanaḥ smṛtaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.16"><label xml:lang="en">4.28.16</label> gavyaṃ payaḥ suvarṇaṃ ca
            madhūcchiṣṭaṃ ca mākṣikam |
            <caesura/>
             pītaṃ śatasahasrābhihutaṃ yuktarathaṃ smṛtam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.17"><label xml:lang="en">4.28.17</label> vacāghṛtasuvarṇaṃ ca bilvacūrṇam
            iti trayam |
            <caesura/>
             medhyam āyuṣyam ārogyapuṣṭisaubhāgyavardhanam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.18"><label xml:lang="en">4.28.18</label> vāsāmūlatulākvāthe tailam āvāpya
            sādhitam |
            <caesura/>
             hutvā sahasram aśnīyān medhyam āyuṣyam ucyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.19"><label xml:lang="en">4.28.19</label> yāvakāṃstāvakān khāded abhibhūya
            yavāṃs tathā |
            <caesura/>
             pippalīmadhusaṃyuktān śikṣā caraṇavad bhavet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.20"><label xml:lang="en">4.28.20</label> madhvāmalakacūrṇāni suvarṇam iti
            ca trayam |
            <caesura/>
             prāśyāriṣṭagṛhīto 'pi mucyate prāṇasaṃśayāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.21"><label xml:lang="en">4.28.21</label> śatāvarīghṛtaṃ samyag upayuktaṃ
            dine dine |
            <caesura/>
             sakṣaudraṃ sasuvarṇaṃ ca narendraṃ sthāpayed vaśe || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.22"><label xml:lang="en">4.28.22</label> gocandanā mohanikā madhukaṃ
            mākṣikaṃ madhu |
            <caesura/>
             suvarṇam iti saṃyogaḥ peyaḥ saubhāgyam icchatā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.23"><label xml:lang="en">4.28.23</label> padmanīlotpalakvāthe
            yaṣṭīmadhukasaṃyute |
            <caesura/>
             sarpir āsāditaṃ gavyaṃ sasuvarṇaṃ sadā pibet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.24"><label xml:lang="en">4.28.24</label> payaś cānupibet siddhaṃ teṣām eva
            samudbhave |
            <caesura/>
             alakṣmīghnaṃ sadā ''āyuṣyaṃ rājyāya subhagāya ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.25"><label xml:lang="en">4.28.25</label> yatra nodīrito mantro yogeṣv eteṣu
            sādhane |
            <caesura/>
             śabditā tatra sarvatra gāyatrī tripadā bhavet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.26"><label xml:lang="en">4.28.26</label> pāpmānaṃ nāśayanty etā dadyuś

            paratantrāvalokanam |

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.28"><label xml:lang="en">4.28.28</label> āyuṣyaṃ bhojanaṃ jīrṇe vegānāṃ
            cāvidhāraṇam |
            <caesura/>
             brahmacaryam ahiṃsā ca sāhasānāṃ ca varjanam ||</l>

        <div n="29" type="adhyāya">
          <head>ekonatriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>
          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.1"><label xml:lang="en">4.29.1</label> athātaḥ
            svabhāvavyādhipratiṣedhanīyaṃ rasāyanaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.2"><label xml:lang="en">4.29.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.3"><label xml:lang="en">4.29.3</label> brahmādayo 'sṛjan pūrvam amṛtaṃ
            somasaṃjñitam |
            <caesura/>
             jarāmṛtyuvināśāya vidhānaṃ tasya vakṣyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.4"><label xml:lang="en">4.29.4</label> eka eva khalu bhagavān somaḥ
            sthānanāmākṛtivīryaviśeṣaiś caturviṃśatidhābhidyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.5"><label xml:lang="en">4.29.5</label> aṃśumān muñjavāṃś caiva candramā
            rajataprabhaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             dūrvāsomaḥ kanīyāṃś ca śvetākṣaḥ kanakaprabhaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.6"><label xml:lang="en">4.29.6</label> pratānavāṃstālavṛntaḥ karavīro
            'ṃśavān api |
            <caesura/>
             svayaṃprabho mahāsomo yaś cāpi garuḍāhṛtaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.7"><label xml:lang="en">4.29.7</label> gāyatras traiṣṭubhaḥ pāṅkto jāgataḥ
            śākvaras tathā |
            <caesura/>
             agniṣṭomo raivataś ca yathokta iti saṃjñitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.8"><label xml:lang="en">4.29.8</label> gāyatryā tripadā yukto yaś coḍupatir
            ucyate |
            <caesura/>
             ete somāḥ samākhyātā vedoktair nām abhiḥ śubhaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.9"><label xml:lang="en">4.29.9</label> sarveṣām eva caiteṣām eko vidhir
            upāsane |
            <caesura/>
             sarve tulyaguṇāś caiva vidhānaṃ teṣu vakṣyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.10"><label xml:lang="en">4.29.10</label> ato 'nyatamaṃ somam upayuyukṣuḥ
            sarvopakaraṇaparicārakopetaḥ praśaste deśe trivṛtam āgāraṃ kārayitvā hṛtadoṣaḥ
            pratisaṃsṛṣṭabhaktaḥ praśasteṣu tithikaraṇamuhūrtanakṣatreṣu aṃśumantam
            ādāyādhvarakalpenāhṛtam abhiṣutam abhihutaṃ cāntarāgāre
            kṛtamaṅgalasvastivācanaḥ somakandaṃ suvarṇasūcyā vidārya payo gṛhṇīyāt
            sauvarṇe (rājate vā) pātre 'ñjalimātraṃ, tataḥ sakṛd evopayuñjīta nāsvādayan,
            tata upaspṛśya śeṣam apsv avasādya yamaniyamābhyām ātmānaṃ saṃyojya vāgyato
            'bhyantarataḥ suhṛdbhir upāsyamāno viharet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.11"><label xml:lang="en">4.29.11</label> rasāyanaṃ pītavāṃs tu nivāte
            tanmanāḥ śuciḥ |
            <caesura/>
             āsīta tiṣṭhet krāmec ca na kathaṃcana saṃviśet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.12"><label xml:lang="en">4.29.12</label> sāyaṃ vā bhuktavān upaśrutaśāntiḥ
            kuśaśayyāyāṃ kṛṣṇājinottarāyāṃ suhṛdbhir upāsyamānaḥ śayīta, tṛṣito vā
            śītodakamātrāṃ pibet (aśanāyito vā kṣīraṃ); tataḥ prātar utthāyopaśrutaśāntiḥ
            kṛtamaṅgalo gāṃ spṛṣṭvā tatahaivāsīta, tasya jīrṇe some chardir utpadyate,
            tataḥ śoṇitāktaṃ kṛmivyāmiśraṃ charditavate sāyaṃ śṛtaśītaṃ kṣīraṃ vitaret;
            tatas tṛtīye 'hani kṛmivyāmiśram atisāryate, sa
            tenāniṣṭapratigrahabhuktaprabhṛtibhir viśeṣair vinirmuktaḥ śuddhatanur
            bhavati, tataḥ sāyaṃ snātāya pūrvavad eva kṣīraṃ vitaret, kṣaumavastrāstṛtāyāṃ
            cainaṃ śayyāyāṃ śāyayet; tataś caturthe 'hani tasya śvayathur utpadyate, tataḥ
            sarvāṅgebhyaḥ kṛmayo niṣkrāmanti, tadahaś ca śayyāyāṃ pāṃśubhir avakīryamāṇaḥ
            śayīta, tataḥ sāyaṃ pūrvavad eva kṣīraṃ vitaret; evaṃ pañcamaṣaṣṭhayor
            divasayor varteta, kevalam ubhayakālam asmai kṣīraṃ vitaret; tataḥ saptame
            'hani nirmāṃsas tv agasthibhūtaḥ kevalaṃ somaparigrahād evocchvasiti, tad ahaś
            ca kṣīreṇa sukhoṣṇena pariṣicya tilamadhukacandanānuliptadehaṃ payaḥ pāyayet;
            tato 'ṣṭame 'hani prātar eva kṣīrapariṣiktaṃ candanapradigdhāgātraṃ payaḥ
            pāyayitvā pāṃśuśayyāṃ samutsṛjya kṣaumavastrāstṛtāyāṃ śayyāyāṃ śāyayet, tato
            'sya māṃsam āpyāyyate, tvak cāvadalati, dantanakharomāṇi cāsya patanti; tasya
            navamadivasāt prabhṛty aṇutailābhyaṅgaḥ somavalkakaṣāyapariṣekaḥ; tato daśame
            'hany etad eva vitaret, tato 'sya tvak sthiratām upaiti; evam
            ekādaśadvādaśayor varteta; tatas trayodaśāt prabhṛti somavalkakaṣāyapariṣekaḥ,
            evam āṣoḍaśād varteta; tataḥ saptadaśāṣṭādaśayor divasayor daśanā jāyante
            śikhariṇaḥ snigdhavajravaidūryasphaṭikaprakāśāḥ samāḥ sthirāḥ sahiṣṇavaḥ, tadā
            prabhṛti cānavaiḥ śālitaṇḍulaiḥ kṣīrayavāgūm upaseveta yāvat pañcaviṃśatiriti;
            tato 'smai dadyāc chālyodanaṃ mṛdūbhayakālaṃ payasā, tato 'sya nakhā jāyante
            vidrumendragopakataruṇādity aprakāśāḥ, sthirāḥ snigdhā lakṣaṇasaṃpannāḥ keśāś
            ca sūkṣmā jāyante, tvak ca nīlotpalātasīpuṣpavaidūryaprakāśā; ūrdhvaṃ ca māsāt
            keśān vāpayet, vāpayitvā cośīracandanakṛṣṇatilakalkaiḥ śiraḥ pradihyāt payasā
            vā snāpayet; tato 'syānantaraṃ saptarātrāt keśā jāyante bhramarāñjananibhāḥ
            kuñcitāḥ sthirāḥ snigdhāḥ; tatas trirātrāt prathamāvasathaparisarān niṣkramya
            muhūrtaṃ sthitvā punar evāntaḥ praviśet, tato 'sya balātailam abhyaṅgārthe
            'vacāryaṃ, yavapiṣṭam udvartanārthe, sukhoṣṇaṃ ca payaḥ pariṣekārthe,
            ajakarṇakaṣāyam utsādanārthe, sośīraṃ kūpodakaṃ snānārthe, candanam
            anulepārthe, āmalakarasavimiśrāś cāsya yūṣasūpavikalpāḥ, kṣīramadhukasiddhaṃ
            ca kṛṣṇatilam avacāraṇārthe, evaṃ daśarātraṃ; tato 'nyad daśarātraṃ dvitīye
            parisare varteta; tatas tṛtīye parisare sthirīkurvann ātmānam anyaddaśarātram
            āsīta, kiñcid ātapapavanān vā seveta, punaś cāntaḥ praviśet, na cātmānam
            ādarśe 'psu vā nirīkṣeta rūpaśālitvāt ; tato 'nyad daśarātraṃ krodhādīn
            pariharet, evaṃ sarveṣām upayogavikalpaḥ | viśeṣatas tu
            vallīpratānakṣupakādayaḥ somā brāhmaṇakṣatriyavaiśyair bhakṣayitavyāḥ | teṣāṃ
            tu pramāṇam ardhacatuṣkamuṣṭayaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.13"><label xml:lang="en">4.29.13</label> aṃśumantaṃ sauvarṇe pātre
            'bhiṣuṇuyāt, candramasaṃ rājate; tāv upayujyāṣṭaguṇam aiśvaryam avāpyeśānaṃ
            devam anupraviśati, śeṣāṃs tu tāmramaye mṛnmaye vā rohite vā carmaṇi vitate;
            śūdravarjaṃ tribhir varṇaiḥ somā upayoktavyāḥ | tataś caturthe māse
            paurṇamāsyāṃ śucau deśe brāhmaṇānarcayitvā kṛtamaṅgalo niṣkramya yathoktaṃ
            vrajed iti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.14"><label xml:lang="en">4.29.14</label> oṣadhīnāṃ patiṃ somam upayujya
            vicakṣaṇaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             daśavarṣasahasrāṇi navāṃ dhārayate tanum || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.15"><label xml:lang="en">4.29.15</label> nāgnir na toyaṃ na viṣaṃ na
            śastraṃ nāstram eva ca |
            <caesura/>
             tasyālam āyuḥkṣapaṇe samarthāni bhavanti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.16"><label xml:lang="en">4.29.16</label> bhadrāṇāṃ ṣaṣṭivarṣāṇāṃ
            prasrutānām anekadhā |
            <caesura/>
             kuñjarāṇāṃ sahasrasya balaṃ samadhigacchati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.17"><label xml:lang="en">4.29.17</label> kṣīrodaṃ śakrasadanam uttarāṃś ca
            kurūn api |
            <caesura/>
             yatrecchati sa gantuṃ vā tatrāpratihatā gatiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.18"><label xml:lang="en">4.29.18</label> kandarpa iva rūpeṇa kāntyā candra
            ivāparaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             prahlādayati bhūtānāṃ manāṃsi sa mahādyutiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.19"><label xml:lang="en">4.29.19</label> sāṅgopāṅgāṃś ca nikhilān vedān
            vindati tattvataḥ |
            <caesura/>
             caraty amoghasaṅkalpo devavac cākhilaṃ jagat || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.20"><label xml:lang="en">4.29.20</label> sarveṣām eva somānāṃ patrāṇi daśa
            pañca ca |
            <caesura/>
             tāni śukle ca kṛṣṇe ca jāyante nipatanti ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.21"><label xml:lang="en">4.29.21</label> ekaikaṃ jāyate patraṃ
            somasyāharahas tadā |
            <caesura/>
             śuklasya paurṇamāsyāṃ tu bhavet pañcadaśacchadaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.22"><label xml:lang="en">4.29.22</label> śīryate patram ekaikaṃ divase
            divase punaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             kṛṣṇapakṣakṣaye cāpi latā bhavati kevalā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.23"><label xml:lang="en">4.29.23</label> aṃśumān ājyagandhas tu kandavān
            rajataprabhaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             kadalyākārakandas tu muñjavāṃ llaśunacchadaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.24"><label xml:lang="en">4.29.24</label> candramāḥ kanakābhāso jale carati
            sarvadā |
            <caesura/>
             garuḍāhṛtanāmā ca śvetākṣaś cāpi pāṇḍurau || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.25"><label xml:lang="en">4.29.25</label> sarpanirmokasadṛśau tau
            vṛkṣāgrāvalambinau |
            <caesura/>
             tathā 'nye maṇḍalaiś citraiś citritā iva bhānti te || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.26"><label xml:lang="en">4.29.26</label> sarva eva tu vijñeyāḥ somāḥ
            pañcadaśacchadāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             kṣīrakandalatāvantaḥ patrair nānāvidhaiḥ smṛtāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.27"><label xml:lang="en">4.29.27</label> himavaty arbude sahye mahendre
            malaye tathā |
            <caesura/>
             śrīparvate devagirau girau devasahe tathā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.28"><label xml:lang="en">4.29.28</label> pāriyātre ca vindhye ca devasunde
            hrade tathā |
            <caesura/>
             uttareṇa vitastāyāḥ pravṛddhā ye mahīdharāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.29"><label xml:lang="en">4.29.29</label> haṣṭhavat plavate tatra candramāḥ
            somasattamaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             tasyoddeśeṣu cāpy anti muñjavān aṃśumān api || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.30"><label xml:lang="en">4.29.30</label> tasyoddeśeṣu cāpy asti
            muñjavānaṃśumān api |
            <caesura/>
             kāśmīreṣu saro divyaṃ nāmnā kṣudrakamānasam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.31"><label xml:lang="en">4.29.31</label> gāyatras traiṣṭubhaḥ pāṅkto
            jāgataḥ śākvaras tathā |
            <caesura/>
             atra santy apare cāpi somāḥ somasamaprabhāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.32"><label xml:lang="en">4.29.32</label> yaiś cātra mandabhāgyais te
            bhiṣajaś cāpamānitāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             na tān paśyanty adharmiṣṭhāḥ kṛtaghnāś cāpi mānavāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             bheṣajadveṣiṇaś cāpi brāhmaṇadveṣiṇas tathā ||</l>

          <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ cikitsāsthāne
            svabhāvavyādhipratiṣedhanīyaṃ rasāyanacikitsitaṃ nāmaikonatriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||29
            ||</p>
        </div>

        <div n="30" type="level2" subtype="adhyāya">
          <head>triṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ|</head>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.30.1"><label xml:lang="en">4.30.1</label> athāto nivṛttasantāpīyaṃ rasāyanaṃ
            vyākhyāsyāmaḥ|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.30.2"><label xml:lang="en">4.30.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.30.3"><label xml:lang="en">4.30.3</label> yathā nivṛttasantāpā modante divi
            devatāḥ| tathauṣadhīrimāḥ prāpya modante bhuvi mānavāḥ|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.30.4"><label xml:lang="en">4.30.4</label> atha khalu sapta puruṣā rasāyanaṃ
            nopayuñjīran; tad yathā anātmavānalaso daridraḥ pramādī vyasanīpāpakṛd
            bheṣajāpamānī ceti| saptabhir eva kāraṇairna saṃpadyate; tad yathā
            ajñānādanārambhādasthiracittatvād dāridvyādanāyattatvād
            adharmādauṣadhālābhācceti|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.30.5"><label xml:lang="en">4.30.5</label> athauṣadhīvyākhyāsyāmaḥ tatrājagarī,
            śvetakāpotī, kṛṣṇakāpotī, gonasī, vārāhī, kanyā, chatrā, aticchatrā, kareṇuḥ,
            ajā, cakrakā, ādity aparṇī, brahmasuvarcalā, śrāvaṇī, mahāśrāvaṇī, golomī,
            ajalomī, mahāvegavatī, cetyaṣṭādaśa somasamavīryā mahauṣadhayo vyākhyātāḥ|
            tāsāṃ somavat kriyāśīḥstutayaḥ śāstre+abhihitāḥ| tāsāmāgāre+abhihutānāṃ yāḥ
            kṣīravatyastāsāṃ kṣīrakuḍavaṃ sakṛdevopayuñjīta, yāstvakṣīrā mūlavatyastāsāṃ
            pradeśinīpramāṇāni trīṇi kāṇḍāni pramāṇam upayoge, śvetakāpotī samūlapatrā
            bhakṣayitavyā, gonasyajagarīkṛṣṇakāpotīnāṃ sanakhamuṣṭiṃ khaṇḍaśaḥ kalpayitvā
            kṣīreṇa vipācya parisrāvyābhighāritamabhihutaṃ ca sakṛdevopayuñjīta,
            cakrakāyāḥ payaḥ sakṛdeva, brahmasuvarcalā saptarātram upayoktavyā
            bhakṣyakalpena, śeṣāṇāṃ pañca pañca palāni kṣīrāḍhakakvathitāni
            prasthe+avaśiṣṭe+avatārya parisrāvya sakṛdevopayuñjīta| somavadāhāravihārau
            vyākhyātau, kevalaṃ navanītamabhyaṅgārthe, śeṣaṃ somavadānirgamāditi|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.30.6"><label xml:lang="en">4.30.6</label> bhavanti cātra yuvānaṃ
            siṃhavikrāntaṃ kāntaṃ śrutanigādinam| kuryuretāḥ krameṇaiva dvisahasrāyuṣaṃ
            naram|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.30.7"><label xml:lang="en">4.30.7</label> aṅgadī kuṇḍalī maulī
            divyasrakcandanāmbaraḥ| caratyamoghasaṅkalpo nabhasyambudadurgame|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.30.8"><label xml:lang="en">4.30.8</label> vrajanti pakṣiṇo yena jalalambāś ca
            toyadāḥ| gatiḥ sauṣadhisiddhasya somasiddhe gatiḥ parā|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.30.9"><label xml:lang="en">4.30.9</label> atha vakṣyāmi vijñānamauṣadhīnāṃ
            pṛthak pṛthak| maṇḍalaiḥ kapilaiścitraiḥ sarpābhā pañcaparṇinī|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.30.10"><label xml:lang="en">4.30.10</label> pañcāratnipramāṇā ca
            vijñeyā+ajagarī budhaiḥ| niṣpatrā kanakābhāsā mūle dvyaṅgulasaṃmitā|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.30.11"><label xml:lang="en">4.30.11</label> sarpākārā lohitāntā
            śvetakāpotirucyate| dviparṇinīṃ mūlabhavāmaruṇāṃ kṛṣṇamaṇḍalām|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.30.12"><label xml:lang="en">4.30.12</label> dvyaratnimātrāṃ jānīyād gonasīṃ
            gonasākṛtim| sakṣīrāṃ romaśāṃ mṛdvīṃ rasenekṣurasopamām|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.30.13"><label xml:lang="en">4.30.13</label> evaṃrūparasāṃ cāpi
            kṛṣṇakāpotimādiśet| kṛṣṇasarpasvarūpeṇa vārāhī kandasaṃbhavā|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.30.14"><label xml:lang="en">4.30.14</label> ekapatrā mahāvīryā
            bhinnāñjanasamaprabhā| chatrāticchatrake vidyādrakṣoghne kandasaṃbhave|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.30.15"><label xml:lang="en">4.30.15</label> jarāmṛtyunivāriṇyau
            śvetakāpotisaṃsthite| kāntairdvādaśabhiḥ patrairmayūrāṅgaruhopamaiḥ|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.30.16"><label xml:lang="en">4.30.16</label> kandajā kāñcanakṣīrī kanyā nāma
            mahauṣadhī| kareṇuḥ subahukṣīrā kandena gajarūpiṇī|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.30.17"><label xml:lang="en">4.30.17</label> hastikarṇapalāśasya tulyaparṇā
            dviparṇinī| ajāstanābhakandā tu sakṣīrā śruparūpiṇī|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.30.18"><label xml:lang="en">4.30.18</label> ajā mahauṣadhī jñeyā
            śaṅkhakundendupāṇḍurā| śvetāṃ vicitrakusumāṃ kākādanyā samāṃ kṣupām|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.30.19"><label xml:lang="en">4.30.19</label> cakrakāmoṣadhīṃ
            vidyājjarāmṛtyunivāriṇīm| mūlinī pañcabhiḥ patraiḥ suraktāṃśukakomalaiḥ|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.30.20"><label xml:lang="en">4.30.20</label> ādity aparṇinī jñeyā sadā++ādity
            ānuvartinī| kanakābhā jalānteṣu sarvataḥ parisarpati|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.30.21"><label xml:lang="en">4.30.21</label> sakṣīrā padminīprakhyā devī
            brahmasuvarcalā| aratnimātrakṣupakā patrairdvyaṅgulasaṃmitaiḥ|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.30.22"><label xml:lang="en">4.30.22</label> puṣpairnīlotpalākāraiḥ phalaiś
            cāñjanasannibhaiḥ| śrāvaṇī mahatī jñeyā kanakābhā payasvinī|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.30.23"><label xml:lang="en">4.30.23</label> śrāvaṇī pāṇḍurābhāsā
            mahāśrāvaṇilakṣaṇā| golomī cājalomī ca romaśe kandasaṃbhave|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.30.24"><label xml:lang="en">4.30.24</label> haṃsapādīva vicchinnaiḥ
            patrairmūlasamudbhavaiḥ| athavā śaṅkhapuṣpyā ca samānā sarvarūpataḥ|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.30.25"><label xml:lang="en">4.30.25</label> vetena mahatā++āviṣṭā
            sarpanirmokasannibhā| eṣā vegavatī nāma jāyate hy ambudakṣaye|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.30.26"><label xml:lang="en">4.30.26</label> saptādau sarparūpiṇyo hy auṣadhyo
            yāḥ prakīrtitāḥ| tāsāmuddharaṇaṃ kāryaṃ mantreṇānena sarvadā|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.30.27"><label xml:lang="en">4.30.27</label> mahendrarāmakṛṣṇānāṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ
            gavāmapi| tapasā tejasā vā+api praśāmyadhvaṃ śivāya vai|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.30.28"><label xml:lang="en">4.30.28</label> natreṇānena matimān sarvā
            evābhimantrayet| aśraddadhānairalasaiḥ kṛtaghnaiḥ pāpakarmabhiḥ|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.30.29"><label xml:lang="en">4.30.29</label> naivāsādayituṃ śakyāḥ somāḥ
            somasamāstathā| pītāvaśeṣamamṛtaṃ devairbrahmapurogamaiḥ|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.30.30"><label xml:lang="en">4.30.30</label> nihitaṃ somavīryāsu some cāpy
            oṣadhīpatau| devasunde hradavare tathā sindhau mahānade|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.30.31"><label xml:lang="en">4.30.31</label> dṛśyate ca jalānteṣu medhyā
            brahmasuvarcalā| ādity aparṇinī jñeyā tathaiva himasaṃkṣaye|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.30.32"><label xml:lang="en">4.30.32</label> dṛśyate+ajagarī nityaṃ gonasī
            cāmbudāgame| kāśmīreṣu saro divyaṃ nāmnā kṣudrakamānasam|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.30.33"><label xml:lang="en">4.30.33</label> kareṇus tatra kanyā ca
            chatrāticchatrake tathā| golomī cājalomī ca mahatī śrāvaṇī tathā|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.30.34"><label xml:lang="en">4.30.34</label> vasante kṛṣṇasarpākhyā gonasī ca
            pradṛśyate| kauśikīṃ saritaṃ tīrtvā sañjayanty ās tu pūrvataḥ|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.30.35"><label xml:lang="en">4.30.35</label> kṣitipradeśo valmīkairācito
            yojanatrayam| vijñeyā tatra kāpotī śvetā valmīkamūrdhasu|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.30.36"><label xml:lang="en">4.30.36</label> malaye nalasetau ca
            vegavatyauṣadhī dhruvā| kārtikyāṃ paurṇamāsyāṃ ca bhakṣayettāmupoṣitaḥ|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.30.37"><label xml:lang="en">4.30.37</label> somavaccātra varteta phalaṃ tāvac
            ca kīrtitam| sarvā viceyāstvopadhyaḥ somāś cāpy arbude girau|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.30.38"><label xml:lang="en">4.30.38</label> sa
            śṛṅgairdevacaritairambudānīkabhedibhiḥ| vyāptastīrthaiś ca vikhyātaiḥ
            siddharṣisurasevitaiḥ|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.30.39"><label xml:lang="en">4.30.39</label> guhābhir bhīmarūpābhiḥ
            siṃhonnāditakukṣibhiḥ| vividhairdhātubhiścitraiḥ sarvatraivopaśobhitaḥ|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.30.40"><label xml:lang="en">4.30.40</label> nadīṣu śaileṣu saraḥsu cāpi
            puṇyeṣv araṇyeṣu tathā++āśrameṣu| sarvatra sarvāḥ parimārgitavyāḥ sarvatra
            bhūmirhi vasūni dhatte||</l>
          <trailer>iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ cikitsāsthāne nivṛttasaṃtāpīyaṃ rasāyanaṃ nāma
            triṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||30||</trailer>
